}.tdi_77_fff a:hover{\r\n\t\t\t        color: #444444;\r\n\t\t        }\n\n/* landscape */\n@media (min-width: 1019px) and (max-width: 1140px){\n.tdi_77_fff .tdb-block-inner blockquote p{\r\n\t\t\t (max-width: 1018px){\n.tdi_77_fff,\r\n                .tdi_77_fff > p{\r\n\t\t\t        font-family:Open Sans !important;font-size:13px !important;line-height:1.4 !important;\r\n\t\t    margin-top: 1px;\r\n\t\t\t        line-height: 18.2px !important;\r\n\t\t        }.tdi_77_fff .tdb-block-inner blockquote p{\r\n\t\t\t        font-family:Open Sans !important;font-size:36px !important;line-height:1.1 !important;text-transform:none !important;\r\n\t\t        }\n}\n\n/* phone */\n@media (max-width: 767px){\n.tdi_77_fff,\r\n                .tdi_77_fff > p{\r\n\t\t\t        font-family:Open Sans !important;font-size:13px !important;line-height:1.8 !important;\r\n\t\t        }.tdi_77_fff li{\r\n\t\t\t        font-family:Open Sans !important;font-size:13px !important;line-height:1.4 !important;font-style:normal !important;\r\n\t\t        }.tdi_77_fff li:before{\r\n\t\t\t\t    margin-top: 1px;\r\n\t\t\t        line-height: 18.2px !important;\r\n\t\t        }.tdi_77_fff .tdb-block-inner blockquote p{\r\n\t\t\t        font-family:Open Sans !important;font-size:16px !important;line-height:1.1 !important;text-transform:none !important;\r\n\t\t        }\n}\n</style><div class="tdb-block-inner td-fix-index">\n<p>So, we are currently day 16 into our lockdown. But let me go back a couple of weeks for this one. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>It was going to be tough being restricted to one outdoor form of exercise a day and only leaving the house for one of two reasons, to obtain food, or for medical reasons. So, it was just over two weeks ago that I was expecting my latest dose of steroids into the spine to help elevate the debilitating pain I endure due to my many health issues. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Half expecting the procedure to be cancelled as many (if not all) private hospitals were going to be &#8216;swallowed&#8217; up by the NHS to help ease the frontline. It got to the morning of the procedure and a quick call confirmed that the procedure was currently going ahead. Winner! I have been really suffering these past few weeks and was in real need of having this done.</p>\n\n\n\n<blockquote class="wp-block-quote has-text-align-left"><p>I was laying there, then all of a sudden he hit the spine. Not once, not twice, but too many times</p></blockquote>\n\n\n\n<p>All gowned up, ready to go, just needing the be marked up and were good to go. Thankfully, I was first on the list. So many times now I have been 3rd or 4th and left waiting for 3 hours or more. Today, was much quieter. Then you can hear Ze German from around the corner. Round comes Dr. Weber, I have been in his care now for well over 2 years so totally get his humour. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img src="https://www.lookatourworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/LAOW-1-576x1024.jpeg" alt="" class="wp-image-20717" srcset="https://www.lookatourworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/LAOW-1-576x1024.jpeg 576w, https://www.lookatourworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/LAOW-1-169x300.jpeg 169w, https://www.lookatourworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/LAOW-1-768x1366.jpeg 768w, https://www.lookatourworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/LAOW-1-696x1238.jpeg 696w, https://www.lookatourworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/LAOW-1-236x420.jpeg 236w, https://www.lookatourworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/LAOW-1-600x1067.jpeg 600w, https://www.lookatourworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/LAOW-1.jpeg 800w" sizes="(max-width: 576px) 100vw, 576px" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Walks up to me, picks up my notes and proceeds to tell me some information that could change the way things were going to go.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>To cut a very long dialogue short, there has been some evidence to show that by having this injection can lower my immune system and leave my more susceptible to catching COVID-19 (better known as the Coronavirus). This left me incredibly conflicted, do I go ahead and have the chance to relieve this pain I have 24/7. Or, do I postpone the surgery for an unknown amount of time while this virus fucks off!</p>\n\n\n\n<p>You can see from above, I proceeded with the procedure and after 20 minutes I was out and sipping a hot chocolate and dunking some hobnob-esque biscuits. Now, needing to self-isolate for 12 weeks to minimise the risk of contracting COVID-19.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>15 days in, and I&#8217;m very much still recovering from the injections. Lets hope in a short while to come that things start to improve and I can my mental state can begin to improve as much as possible.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Check back for more lockdown antics next time.</p>\n</div></div><div class="td_block_wrap tdb_single_post_share tdi_78_45f td-pb-border-top td_block_template_13"  data-td-block-uid="tdi_78_45f" >\n<style>\n\n/* inline tdc_css att
